## How It Works

### Set Branding

Upload your brand assets including logo, color scheme, and fonts. Emailgic will automatically maintain brand consistency across all designs.

Your browser does not support the video tag.

### Input Content

Compose your email copy - no layout worries needed. Focus entirely on crafting your message while we handle the design magic.

Your browser does not support the video tag.

### AI Magic

Emailgic analyzes your content and brand elements to generate a professional email design, including AI-generated images that perfectly match your copy. From typography to spacing, every detail is optimized for visual impact.

Your browser does not support the video tag.

### Export

Get production-ready HTML code that works flawlessly across all major email clients. Need changes? Easily modify and regenerate your design anytime.

Your browser does not support the video tag.

## Frequently Asked Questions

### Do I need design skills to use Emailgic?

No, you do not need any design skills. Emailgic uses AI to handle all design work, so anyone can create professional-looking email templates.

### Why use Emailgic instead of directly using ChatGPT to write email templates?

While ChatGPT can generate both text and code, it cannot ensure that the generated code is fully compatible with all email clients. Emailgic, on the other hand, combines your content with professional, visually optimized designs tailored to your brand, delivering responsive and client-compatible email layouts without additional design or coding work‚Äã.

### How does Emailgic create unique email designs?

Emailgic's AI analyzes your content and brand elements to generate unique email designs. It does not rely on generic templates, ensuring every email is tailor-made. The AI is trained on top-notch email designs.

### Can I use my own brand elements with Emailgic?

Emailgic has a multi-branding feature that allows you to switch between different brand styles within the same account. You can set up predefined brand elements (logos, colors, fonts) for each brand, saving time and effort.

### Is the HTML code generated by Emailgic compatible with all email clients?

Yes, Emailgic ensures compatibility with all major email clients. The production-ready HTML code works flawlessly across various platforms.

### Can I modify the designs generated by Emailgic?

Yes, you can easily tweak any element or ask the AI to redesign. Emailgic provides an intuitive interface that allows users to customize layouts, fonts, and colors.

### How does Emailgic ensure my emails look good on all devices?

Emailgic ensures responsive design, meaning your emails display perfectly on any screen, whether it's a smartphone, tablet, or desktop. It guarantees a flawless design across all devices.

### How does Emailgic handle image selection for my emails?

Emailgic automatically recommends and generates images based on the email's content. This feature enhances visual appeal and helps drive brand engagement. The AI selects images that match your copy.

### Is my data secure with Emailgic?

Yes, your content and assets are encrypted and used only for generating your designs. Emailgic never shares your data.

### What kind of users can benefit from using Emailgic?

Emailgic is useful for startups, SMBs, marketing teams, e-commerce businesses, content creators, freelancers, consultants, and anyone who needs professional emails without design resources. It helps enhance design efficiency and improve the overall effectiveness of your emails.
